< Review>
My family and I ate here since 2008 when we moved to Lemon Grove. The food was delicious but the man working the front counter always made us come back. Once he recognized us as regulars, he would ask how we are doing and seemed like he really cared for us. Even when we moved away, we always came back to this restaurant because we consider the food here our comfort food. It breaks my heart seeing this place closed since covid hit. I just want you to know that I hope you and your family is doing well.< /Review>

<date>1617123612477<//date><rating>5< /rating>< review>
My family I used to eat here and enjoyed the food.  I love their shrimp and snow peas, Terriyaki and/or Lemon Chicken, Beef with broccoli, etc.  Not to mention, they even serve Viatnamese and Japanese food as well as Chinese food.  They serve delicious and nutritious food.  Plus, the prices were reasonable.  Unfortunately, this place is out of business thanks to COVID-19.  I wish this place was back in business.  This place is a gem in Lemon Grove.</review>

< text>
2021/02/28

I ordered here via BeyondMenu and I am saddened that quality control slipped to a 3 out of 10 stars.

I ordered two appetizers and two entrees.  One entree was incorrect (right dish, wrong protein) and the appetizers ..well let's say more care could have gone into the food prep.

There were shells present in the shrimp entree. (When, I ordered Kung-Pao Chicken).

The BBQ pork fried rice had huge chunks of fat and tendon sitting in it .. and there was no bbq to be found.  and the fried rice was a bit scorched this time around.

The fried shrimp appetizer .. had clearly been fried hours ahead of time based on the fact that it was served at room temperature, and rock hard.

It is really a shame, that service was absymal enough that I am here posting this.  Normally Panda-house is our "Go-to" place for easy Chinese takeout.  But this left a bad taste in our mouth's.   Figuratively and Literally.</text>

<Rate>4<//Rate>< text>
I got the BBQ Pork Chow Fun, wife got Sweet & Sour Chicken.  Both were excellent.  While it is obvious that they maintain a cleaning regimen for the floor, tables, and chairs (even the ceiling fans were clean), they miss a lot, making the place a bit uncomfortable.  There were obvious splashes of food/juice on the wall paneling above some of the tables, and a very grimy baseboard-to-floor area.  The whole place could use a good scrubbing and new paint.  We will go again, but probably take-out rather than eat-in.< /text>

<user>117940759074438002341<//user><username>Angelica Ferreira</username><Time>1508115832721< /Time><rate>5<//rate><Review>Panda Resturant is our go to place for the BEST teriyaki chicken in San Diego. The chicken is pan seared on the outside and moist on the inside. The sauce is savory in the sweeter side and really makes the chicken complete. This also comes with the freshest veggies and a side of white rice. I highly recommend ordering this! Depending on if you are ordering a small or a large the prices range from $7-$9 but can feed 2 people!

My equally favorite item to order here are the chicken and pork banh mi sandwiches. It included picked cucumber, carrots, daikon, and sweet grilled onions, cilantro and pepper to top it off! Beware of the jalepenos! Those are hot for me but really give it a kick.

I usually stick to these items, but their chow mein is also very tasty. And my mom loves their won ton soup.

If you are in the area stopping here is a must! This restaurant doesn't get a ton of people that eat in and is mainly delivery or pick up. Don and his brother are very friendly and we love coming here!!!</Review><Pictures>None</Pictures>< resp>

<Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
First visit was fine. Ordered the gyro and enjoyed it with no issues. Second visit was a bit more frustrating. Ordered chicken shawarma and sat down to wait. Staff dropped it off to the adjacent table who ordered after me even after making an attempt to let them know they are dropping my plate off to the wrong table. I let the staff know at the front that I believe they made a mistake, no big deal.

Front staff says "Oh no worries there is another one coming up." Cool, guess I'll wait a little longer. Sit back down and a few minutes later staff is bringing more food to the table next to me, the same one that ordered after me. Keep in mind they are a larger party. I'm just here on my lunch break trying to eat and get back to work. Feels bad to see a large party get served before a single order especially since they came in after I did.

This table looks at the food they're brought and say "Hey, I ordered the kebab not the shawarma." Hmm... I'm still patiently waiting, hoping they bring me my food soon. Staff starts heading my way, drops off chicken kebab, and says "Hey you were right, I accidentally gave your food to the other table." This is the part that kind of turned the whole thing sour, the gentlemen helping me turns around to walk back to the counter after acknowledging he gave my order away and then dropping off the other tables order in front of me. I had to stop him and ask if I could get the order I wanted.

Best part here, after waiting even longer, they bring my order out... to the other table.

Food is great, service seems...inconsistent. I'd probably go back, but not for a while. Maybe the staff needs some more training or experience to give customers a more consistent experience.<//Review>

< Text>
I have been struggling with hyperpigmentation and melasma for years. I don‚Äôt like the look of applying layers of  foundation or concealer to cover brown spots. I have tried many laser treatments, chemical peels, and skin care regimens. After my initial consultation at Skin Perfect I decided to try the Cosmelan Peel. Rachel was amazing!

Treatment: The first day she applied the Cosmelan mask treatment, which was similar to a mud mask that you wear for 10-hours and rinse off before bed. You don‚Äôt apply anything the next two days. By the third day I started to peel. That is when you start applying the at-home treatment both morning and night. It is very similar to a medium colored foundation. My face peeled around the forehead, cheeks, and chin area for the first week. I stayed indoors most of the time the first week. The second week had slight peeling, and seemed more dry around the chin and upper lip area. By the end of week two I went in for my follow up appt, which also consisted of an oxygen facial, my results were significantly noticeable. My skin had such an amazing glow to it. I did not need to wear any make up and it only appeared dry when wearing the at home product throughout the day. I bought a hydrating facial spritzer that I used every two hours to prevent the dryness from being noticeable. At one month you go in for another mask that you wear all day, exactly like the initial mask. The peeling and dryness was a lot less. After another two weeks you follow up with another oxygen facial and that‚Äôs when you notice the entire results. My pigmentation was gone, and my texture and pore size benefited from this treatment. I am extremely happy with the results. My only regret is not doing this a long time ago. If you can commit to the entire process; 10-hour mask for the first day, at home application morning and night for two weeks (without skipping), oxygen facials and follow up appts, second mask (all which is included in the price), and deal with the peeling (yes it will be noticeable for at least the first week or two), then you will have the best results.</Text>

< Name>
Martin Cremer<//Name>
<time>1543703175916< /time>< rate>
5</rate>
<review>This drone repair shop is an excellent resource for both professionals and hobbyist alike. If one has a system failure on their drone that cannot be easily remedied, this is your place. The flat ribbon cable which extends from the back of the camera and up to the mother board was torn. I ordered a replacement cable on amazon and attempted the repair. Damage to this cable is a common problem. Therefore, there are plenty of videos demonstrating how to fix the issue in a step by step fashion. Many of these videos contain a disclaimer that the repair can be challenging. I am generally all for learning how to fix things on one's own, however, this particular repair involves removing extremely delicate components essential to overall drone functionality. Further, the various screws and cable interfaces seem to grow infinitesimally small as you progress! The most challenging step of this repair is folding the ribbon cable and threading it correctly on the gimbal assembly. It's oragami from hell! This was a maddening experience for me. If you want to learn how complex the Mavic Pro is or if you are skilled working with practically invisible parts and peices by all means proceed with the DIY repair. If you're in the least bit reluctant spare yourself the agony and get the drone fixed by professionals.

I explained the issue that I had with the drone over the phone with the shop owner Ludwig. He gave me an approximate estimate but insisted that it had to be inspected. I finally went in to get a diagnosis and the final quote was square in the middle of the initial estimate. I think it's a fair price given how frustrating the job can be. I brought the drone in on a Friday at 2pm and the entire repair was completed within an hour. I wouldn't anticipate such a rapid fix as every job is different, but it seems that fast turnaround is one of the major benefits of coming here.

I brought my drone home on Friday and performed a basic flight test after updating the firmware. The drone was drifting a bit and so I called up the shop. Ludwig suggested that I calibrate the compass (I think he told me to do so when I picked it up). Alas, my Mavic is flying like a dream and I am a happy man. If you're a DJI owner in the Los Angeles area you're very fortunate to have this shop as a resource. I will be coming here for any future needs.</review>< pictures>
None<//pictures>
